USE [Hospital]
GO

/* AppointMent Info Table */

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[appointmentinfo](
	[patid] [int] NULL,
	[apptid] [int] NOT NULL,
	[appdate] [date] NULL,
	[operatory] [int] NULL,
	[provider] [int] NULL,
	[apptime] [time](7) NULL,
	[applength] [numeric](18, 2) NULL,
	[amount] [numeric](18, 2) NULL,
	[clinicid] [int] NULL,
PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[apptid] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

/* Clinic Info table */

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[clinicinfo](
	[clinicid] [int] NOT NULL,
	[clinicname] [varchar](50) NULL,
	[city] [varchar](50) NULL,
	[state] [varchar](50) NULL,
PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[clinicid] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]


/*  Doctor info table */

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[doctorinfo](
	[IDNo] [int] NOT NULL,
	[lastname] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[firstname] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[city] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[state] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[clinicid] [int] NULL
) ON [PRIMARY]

/*   patient information */

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[patientinfo](
	[patId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[practiceid] [int] NULL,
	[lastname] [varchar](30) NULL,
	[firstname] [varchar](30) NULL,
	[city] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[state] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[gender] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[patientagegroup] [varchar](20) NULL,
	[birthdate] [date] NULL,
	[age] [int] NULL,
PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[patId] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

/*  Transaction Info */

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[transactioninfo](
	[transid] [int] NOT NULL,
	[patid] [int] NULL,
	[proceduretype] [varchar](50) NULL,
	[proceduredate] [date] NULL,
	[prov] [int] NULL,
	[amount] [numeric](18, 2) NULL,
	[clinicid] [int] NULL,
PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[transid] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
